â”‚   â”‚   | # Portfolio Blog Starter
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | This is a porfolio site template complete with a blog. Includes:
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | - MDX and Markdown support
â”‚   â”‚   | - Optimized for SEO (sitemap, robots, JSON-LD schema)
â”‚   â”‚   | - RSS Feed
â”‚   â”‚   | - Dynamic OG images
â”‚   â”‚   | - Syntax highlighting
â”‚   â”‚   | - Tailwind v4
â”‚   â”‚   | - Vercel Speed Insights / Web Analytics
â”‚   â”‚   | - Geist font
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | ## Demo
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | https://portfolio-blog-starter.vercel.app
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | ## How to Use
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | You can choose from one of the following two methods to use this repository:
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | ### One-Click Deploy
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | Deploy the example using [Vercel](https://vercel.com?utm_source=github&utm_medium=readme&utm_campaign=vercel-examples):
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | [![Deploy with Vercel](https://vercel.com/button)](https://vercel.com/new/clone?repository-url=https://github.com/vercel/examples/tree/main/solutions/blog&project-name=blog&repository-name=blog)
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | ### Clone and Deploy
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | Execute [`create-next-app`](https://github.com/vercel/next.js/tree/canary/packages/create-next-app) with [pnpm](https://pnpm.io/installation) to bootstrap the example:
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | ```bash
â”‚   â”‚   | pnpm create next-app --example https://github.com/vercel/examples/tree/main/solutions/blog blog
â”‚   â”‚   | ```
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | Then, run Next.js in development mode:
â”‚   â”‚   |

â”‚   â”‚   | ```
â”‚   â”‚   |

â”‚   â”‚   | def print_directory_structure(startpath, output_file=None):
â”‚   â”‚   |     """
â”‚   â”‚   |     Recursively prints directory structure with file contents.
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     Args:
â”‚   â”‚   |         startpath (str): Root directory to scan
â”‚   â”‚   |         output_file (str, optional): File to write output to. Defaults to None (prints to console).
â”‚   â”‚   |     """
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     output_stream = None
â”‚   â”‚   |     if output_file:
â”‚   â”‚   |         try:
â”‚   â”‚   |             # Open file with UTF-8 encoding for broad compatibility
â”‚   â”‚   |             output_stream = open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8')
â”‚   â”‚   |         except IOError as e:
â”‚   â”‚   |             print(f"Error opening output file '{output_file}': {e}")
â”‚   â”‚   |             return
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     def write_output(text):
â”‚   â”‚   |         if output_stream:
â”‚   â”‚   |             output_stream.write(text + '\n')
â”‚   â”‚   |         else:
â”‚   â”‚   |             print(text)
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     # Normalize startpath for clean relative path calculations
â”‚   â”‚   |     startpath = os.path.abspath(startpath)
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     write_output(f"Project Structure and Content for: {os.path.basename(startpath)}")
â”‚   â”‚   |     write_output("=" * 60 + "\n")
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |     for root, dirs, files in os.walk(startpath):
â”‚   â”‚   |         # Exclude directories in-place
â”‚   â”‚   |         dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if d not in EXCLUDE_DIRS]
â”‚   â”‚   |         
â”‚   â”‚   |         # Calculate depth level relative to the startpath
â”‚   â”‚   |         relative_root = os.path.relpath(root, startpath)
â”‚   â”‚   |         level = relative_root.count(os.sep) if relative_root != '.' else 0
â”‚   â”‚   |         
â”‚   â”‚   |         # Indentation for the directory name
â”‚   â”‚   |         dir_indent = 'â”‚   ' * level + ('â”œâ”€â”€ ' if level > 0 else '')
â”‚   â”‚   |         
â”‚   â”‚   |         # Print directory name
â”‚   â”‚   |         write_output(f"{dir_indent}{os.path.basename(root)}/")
â”‚   â”‚   |         
â”‚   â”‚   |         # Indentation for file names within this directory
â”‚   â”‚   |         file_indent = 'â”‚   ' * (level + 1) + 'â”œâ”€â”€ '
â”‚   â”‚   |         
â”‚   â”‚   |         for file in files:
â”‚   â”‚   |             if file not in EXCLUDE_FILES:
â”‚   â”‚   |                 file_path = os.path.join(root, file)
â”‚   â”‚   |                 
â”‚   â”‚   |                 # Print file name
â”‚   â”‚   |                 write_output(f"{file_indent}{file}")
â”‚   â”‚   |                 
â”‚   â”‚   |                 # Check if file content should be extracted
â”‚   â”‚   |                 if file_path.lower().endswith(CODE_EXTENSIONS):
â”‚   â”‚   |                     
â”‚   â”‚   |                     # Consistent indentation prefix for content lines
â”‚   â”‚   |                     CONTENT_PREFIX = 'â”‚   ' * (level + 2) + '| ' 
â”‚   â”‚   |                     
â”‚   â”‚   |                     try:
â”‚   â”‚   |                         write_output(f"{CONTENT_PREFIX}--- FILE CONTENT START ({file}) ---")
â”‚   â”‚   |                         
â”‚   â”‚   |                         # Use universal read 'r' with specified encoding
â”‚   â”‚   |                         with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as content_file:
â”‚   â”‚   |                             content = content_file.read()
â”‚   â”‚   |                             
â”‚   â”‚   |                             # Prepend the content prefix to every line
â”‚   â”‚   |                             content_lines = content.split('\n')
â”‚   â”‚   |                             formatted_content = '\n'.join([f"{CONTENT_PREFIX}{line}" for line in content_lines])
â”‚   â”‚   |                             
â”‚   â”‚   |                             write_output(formatted_content)
â”‚   â”‚   |                             
â”‚   â”‚   |                         write_output(f"{CONTENT_PREFIX}--- FILE CONTENT END ---")
â”‚   â”‚   |                         write_output('')  # Empty line after content block
â”‚   â”‚   |                         
â”‚   â”‚   |                     except UnicodeDecodeError:
â”‚   â”‚   |                          write_output(f"{CONTENT_PREFIX}[ERROR READING FILE: Skipping due to non-UTF-8 binary content or encoding issues]")
â”‚   â”‚   |                          write_output('')
â”‚   â”‚   |                     except Exception as e:
â”‚   â”‚   |                         # Handle other errors like permission denied
â”‚   â”‚   |                         write_output(f"{CONTENT_PREFIX}[ERROR READING FILE: {str(e)}]")
â”‚   â”‚   |                         write_output('')
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |     if output_stream:
â”‚   â”‚   |         output_stream.close()
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   | if __name__ == "__main__":
â”‚   â”‚   |     if len(sys.argv) < 2:
â”‚   â”‚   |         print("Usage: python project_code_extractor.py <project_directory> [output_file]")
â”‚   â”‚   |         sys.exit(1)
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     project_dir = sys.argv[1]
â”‚   â”‚   |     output_file = sys.argv[2] if len(sys.argv) > 2 else "code_structure.txt"
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     if not os.path.isdir(project_dir):
â”‚   â”‚   |         print(f"Error: Directory '{project_dir}' does not exist.")
â”‚   â”‚   |         sys.exit(1)
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     print(f"Starting extraction from: {project_dir}")
â”‚   â”‚   |     print_directory_structure(project_dir, output_file)
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     if os.path.exists(output_file):
â”‚   â”‚   |         print(f"Extraction complete. Structure saved to: {output_file}")
â”‚   â”‚   |     else:
â”‚   â”‚   |         print("Extraction failed or output file could not be created.")
â”‚   â”‚   | --- FILE CONTENT END ---

â”‚   â”‚   | --- FILE CONTENT START (robots.ts) ---

â”‚   â”‚   | export async function analyzePlaylistDiscovery(playlistId: string, playlistName: string, artists: string[]) {

â”‚   â”‚   |   if (!access_token) return { error: "No access token" };
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |   const sampleArtists = artists.slice(0, 10);
â”‚   â”‚   |   let discoveryCount = 0;
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |   // Search Context: "Artist Name + Playlist Name"
â”‚   â”‚   |   const checks = await Promise.all(
â”‚   â”‚   |     sampleArtists.map(async (artist) => {
â”‚   â”‚   |       try {
â”‚   â”‚   |         const query = `${artist} ${playlistName}`;
â”‚   â”‚   |         
â”‚   â”‚   |         // Updated limit to 50 (MAX) to catch all possible results
â”‚   â”‚   |         const res = await fetch(
â”‚   â”‚   |           `https://api.spotify.com/v1/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}&type=playlist&limit=50`,
â”‚   â”‚   |           { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${access_token}` } }
â”‚   â”‚   |         );
â”‚   â”‚   |         
â”‚   â”‚   |         const data = await res.json();
â”‚   â”‚   |         return data.playlists?.items || [];
â”‚   â”‚   |       } catch (e) {
â”‚   â”‚   |         console.error(e);
â”‚   â”‚   |         return [];
â”‚   â”‚   |       }
â”‚   â”‚   |     })
â”‚   â”‚   |   );
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |   checks.forEach((searchResults) => {
â”‚   â”‚   |     if (!Array.isArray(searchResults)) return;
â”‚   â”‚   |     
â”‚   â”‚   |     // Filter out nulls
â”‚   â”‚   |     const validResults = searchResults.filter(item => item !== null);
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |     // Check if OUR playlist appears in the results
â”‚   â”‚   |     const isFound = validResults.some((pl: any) => 
â”‚   â”‚   |         pl.id === playlistId || 
â”‚   â”‚   |         (pl.name && pl.name.toLowerCase() === playlistName.toLowerCase())
â”‚   â”‚   |     );
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |     if (isFound) discoveryCount++;
â”‚   â”‚   |   });
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |   // --- SCORING LOGIC ---
â”‚   â”‚   |   
â”‚   â”‚   |   // 1. Calculate Percentage
â”‚   â”‚   |   const percentage = Math.round((discoveryCount / sampleArtists.length) * 100);
â”‚   â”‚   |   
â”‚   â”‚   |   // 2. Discovery Score Logic
â”‚   â”‚   |   // Rule: If percentage is > 70, Score = 100. Otherwise, Score = Percentage.
â”‚   â”‚   |   let score = percentage;
â”‚   â”‚   |   if (percentage > 70) {
â”‚   â”‚   |     score = 100;
â”‚   â”‚   |   }
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |   // 3. Determine Rating Badge
â”‚   â”‚   |   let rating = "Bad ğŸ”»";
â”‚   â”‚   |   if (score >= 70) rating = "Amazing ğŸš€";
â”‚   â”‚   |   else if (score >= 40) rating = "Good ğŸŒŸ";
â”‚   â”‚   |   else if (score >= 10) rating = "Okay ğŸ˜";
â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   |   return {
â”‚   â”‚   |     score,
â”‚   â”‚   |     percentage,
â”‚   â”‚   |     rating,
â”‚   â”‚   |     analyzed_count: sampleArtists.length
â”‚   â”‚   |   };
â”‚   â”‚   | }

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   | // The main component that implements the delayed popup logic
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   | export function DelayedSubscribePopup() {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   const DELAY_TIME_MS = 30000; // 10 seconds
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   useEffect(() => {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     // 1. Set a timer to show the popup
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     const timer = setTimeout(() => {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |       setIsVisible(true);
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     }, DELAY_TIME_MS);
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     // 2. Clear the timeout if the component unmounts (cleanup)
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     return () => clearTimeout(timer);
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   }, []); // Empty dependency array means this runs only once on mount
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   // Optional: Function to close the popup manually
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   const closePopup = () => {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     setIsVisible(false);
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   };
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   if (!isVisible) {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     return null; // Don't render anything if it's not visible
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   }
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   | 
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   return (
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     // Backdrop for the modal
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black bg-opacity-75 p-4" onClick={closePopup}>
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |       
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |       {/* Container for the content, stopping propagation prevents closing when clicking the content */}
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |       <div 
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |         className="relative max-w-xl w-full transform transition-all duration-300 scale-100 opacity-100" 
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |         onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |       >
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |         <SubscribeCTAContent />
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |         
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |         {/* Close button */}
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |         <button
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |           onClick={closePopup}
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |           className="absolute top-2 right-2 text-white hover:text-gray-300 text-2xl font-bold p-1 leading-none transition-colors"
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |           aria-label="Close subscription popup"
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |         >
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |           &times;
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |         </button>
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |       </div>
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |     </div>
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   |   );
